       <tr>
        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">
         <div style="line-height:11pt">
          <b>
           Website
          </b>
          <br/>
          <span class="url">
           <a class="external text" href="http://unasur.int/en" rel="nofollow">
            unasur
            <wbr/>
            .int
            <wbr/>
            /en
           </a>
          </span>
         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <p>
       The
       <b>
        Union of South American Nations
       </b>
       (
       <b>
        USAN
       </b>
       ; Spanish:
       <i>
        <span lang="es">
         Unión de Naciones Suramericanas
        </span>
       </i>
       ,
       <b>
        UNASUR
       </b>
       ; Portuguese:
       <i>
        <span lang="pt">
         União de Nações Sul-Americanas
        </span>
       </i>
       ,
       <b>
        UNASUL
       </b>
       ; Dutch:
       <i>
        <span lang="nl">
         Unie van Zuid-Amerikaanse Naties
        </span>
       </i>
       ,
       <b>
        UZAN
       </b>
       ; and sometimes referred to as the
       <b>
        South American Union
       </b>
       ) is an
       <a href="/wiki/Intergovernmentalism" title="Intergovernmentalism">
        intergovernmental
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Regional_organization" title="Regional organization">
        regional organization
       </a>
       comprising 12 South American countries.
      </p>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/UNASUR_Constitutive_Treaty" title="UNASUR Constitutive Treaty">
        UNASUR Constitutive Treaty
       </a>
       was signed on 23 May 2008, at the Third Summit of Heads of State, held in
       <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">
        Brasília
       </a>
       , Brazil.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bbc2_9-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-bbc2-9">
         [9]
        </a>
       </sup>
       According to the Constitutive Treaty, the Union's headquarters will be located in
       <a href="/wiki/Quito" title="Quito">
        Quito
       </a>
       , Ecuador.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bloomberg1_3-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-bloomberg1-3">
         [3]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On 1 December 2010, Uruguay became the ninth state to ratify the UNASUR treaty, thus giving the union full legality.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-buenosairesherald1_10-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-buenosairesherald1-10">
         [10]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MercoPress2_11-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-MercoPress2-11">
         [11]
        </a>
       </sup>
       As the Constitutive Treaty entered into force on 11 March 2011, UNASUR became a legal entity during a meeting of Foreign Ministers in
       <a href="/wiki/Ciudad_Mitad_del_Mundo" title="Ciudad Mitad del Mundo">
        Mitad del Mundo
       </a>
       , Ecuador, where they had laid the foundation stone for the Secretariat Headquarters.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">
        <a href="#cite_note-12">
         [12]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/South_American_Parliament" title="South American Parliament">
        South American Parliament
       </a>
       will be located in
       <a href="/wiki/Cochabamba" title="Cochabamba">
        Cochabamba
       </a>
       , Bolivia, while the headquarters of its bank, the
       <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_the_South" title="Bank of the South">
        Bank of the South
       </a>
       are located in
       <a href="/wiki/Caracas" title="Caracas">
        Caracas
       </a>
       , Venezuela.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bloomberg1_3-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-bloomberg1-3">
         [3]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 4 May 2010, at a heads of state summit held in
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Campana,_Buenos_Aires_Province" title="Campana, Buenos Aires Province">
        Campana
       </a>
       , 75 km (47 mi) north of
       <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">
        Buenos Aires
       </a>
       , former Argentine President
       <a href="/wiki/N%C3%A9stor_Kirchner" title="Néstor Kirchner">
        Néstor Kirchner
       </a>
       was unanimously elected the first
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Secretary_General_of_UNASUR" title="Secretary General of UNASUR">
        Secretary General of UNASUR
       </a>
       for a two-year term. The new post was conceived as a first step towards the creation of a permanent bureaucratic body for a
       <a href="/wiki/Supranational_union" title="Supranational union">
        supranational union
       </a>
       , which will eventually replace the political bodies of
       <a href="/wiki/Mercosur" title="Mercosur">
        Mercosur
       </a>
       and CAN. The headquarters of the secretariat is located in
       <a href="/wiki/Quito" title="Quito">
        Quito
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       After Argentina, Bolivia, Chile, Ecuador, Guyana, Peru, Suriname and Venezuela, Uruguay became the ninth nation to ratify the constitutive treaty of the organization on 1 December 2010, thus completing the minimum number of ratifications Necessary for the entry into force of the Treaty, on 11 March 2011
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">
        <a href="#cite_note-13">
         [13]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-buenosairesherald1_10-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-buenosairesherald1-10">
         [10]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MercoPress2_11-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-MercoPress2-11">
         [11]
        </a>
       </sup>
       With the entry into force of the Treaty,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">
        <a href="#cite_note-14">
         [14]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Unasur became a legal entity during the Summit Ministers of Foreign Affairs, in
       <a href="/wiki/Ciudad_Mitad_del_Mundo" title="Ciudad Mitad del Mundo">
        Mitad del Mundo
       </a>
       , Ecuador, where the cornerstone was laid for the headquarters of the General Secretariat of the Union.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">
        <a href="#cite_note-15">
         [15]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">
        <a href="#cite_note-16">
         [16]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
      </p>

        <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2">
         <a href="#History">
          <span class="tocnumber">
           2
          </span>
          <span class="toctext">
           History
          </span>
         </a>

      <p>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Overview">
        Overview
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Overview">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       At the
       <a href="/wiki/2004_South_American_Summit" title="2004 South American Summit">
        Third South American Summit
       </a>
       on 8 December 2004, presidents or representatives from 12 South American nations signed the
       <i>
        <a href="/wiki/Cusco_Declaration" title="Cusco Declaration">
         Cusco Declaration
        </a>
       </i>
       , a two-page statement of intent announcing the foundation of the South American Community. Panama and Mexico attended the signing ceremony as observers.
      </p>
      <p>
       The mechanics of the new entity came out of the First South American Community of Nations Heads of State Summit, which was held in Brasília on 29–30 September 2005. An important operating condition of UNASUR is that no new institutions will be created in the first phase, so as not to increase
       <a href="/wiki/Bureaucracy" title="Bureaucracy">
        bureaucracy
       </a>
       , and the community will use the existing institutions belonging to the previous trade blocs.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="History">
        History
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: History">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Background">
        Background
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Background">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation">
       <tr>
        <td class="mbox-image">
         <div style="width:52px">
          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg">
           <img alt="" data-file-height="399" data-file-width="512" height="39" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" width="50"/>
          </a>
         </div>
        </td>
        <td class="mbox-text">
         <div class="mbox-text-span">
          This section
          <b>
           needs additional citations for
           <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">

           </a>
          </b>

         </div>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </table>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Latin_American_integration" title="Latin American integration">
        Latin American integration
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Pan-Americanism" title="Pan-Americanism">
        Pan-Americanism
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_(4).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1311" data-file-width="1967" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_%284%29.jpg/220px-Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_%284%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_%284%29.jpg/330px-Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_%284%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_%284%29.jpg/440px-Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_%284%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Presidentes_de_pa%C3%ADses_da_Am%C3%A9rica_do_Sul_durante_a_primeira_reuni%C3%A3o_do_CASA_(4).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Heads of State of the then South American Community of Nations in
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brasilia" title="Brasilia">
          Brasilia
         </a>
         in September 2005.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Between the 15th and 19th centuries, the
       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_colonization_of_the_Americas" title="Spanish colonization of the Americas">
        Spanish
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_colonization_of_the_Americas" title="Portuguese colonization of the Americas">
        Portuguese
       </a>
       colonization brought about the establishment and development of
       <a href="/wiki/Colonial_empire" title="Colonial empire">
        colonial empires
       </a>
       in the Americas that integrated politically, economically and culturally vast extensions of the continent each with their respective metropolis.
      </p>
      <p>
       Since the
       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_American_wars_of_independence" title="Spanish American wars of independence">
        Spanish American wars of independence
       </a>
       a trend towards the political integration of the newly born republics of
       <a href="/wiki/Hispanic_America" title="Hispanic America">
        Hispanic America
       </a>
       became strong in the thinking of several independence leaders, influenced in turn by the
       <a href="/wiki/Enlightenment_in_Spain" title="Enlightenment in Spain">
        Spanish Enlightenment
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/French_Revolution" title="French Revolution">
        French
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/American_Revolution" title="American Revolution">
        American
       </a>
       revolutions. A notable early exponent of this trend was
       <a href="/wiki/Francisco_de_Miranda" title="Francisco de Miranda">
        Francisco de Miranda
       </a>
       , who envisioned a federated republic encompassing all of Hispanic America, which he called "Colombia".
      </p>
      <p>
       The independence war efforts saw the concurrence of integrated armies composed by Spanish Americans of diverse regions on both sides of the conflict (v.g.
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Patriot_(Spanish_American_Revolution)" title="Patriot (Spanish American Revolution)">
        Patriots
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Royalist_(Spanish_American_Revolution)" title="Royalist (Spanish American Revolution)">
        Royalists
       </a>
       ), and fighting all over the territories of many future nations. For example, the
       <a href="/wiki/Army_of_the_Andes" title="Army of the Andes">
        Army of the Andes
       </a>
       which was gathered in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Provinces_of_the_River_Plate" title="United Provinces of the River Plate">
        United Provinces of the River Plate
       </a>
       fought in
       <a href="/wiki/Chilean_War_of_Independence" title="Chilean War of Independence">
        Chile
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Peruvian_War_of_Independence" title="Peruvian War of Independence">
        Peru
       </a>
       and Ecuador, and later integrated with
       <a href="/wiki/Military_career_of_Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar" title="Military career of Simón Bolívar">
        Simón Bolívar's Army
       </a>
       (which itself included troops of future Venezuela, Colombia and Ecuador) to further fight in Peru and the
       <a href="/wiki/Upper_Peru" title="Upper Peru">
        Upper Peru
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       By the 1820s, the main proponent of a federation of the newly born republics was
       <a href="/wiki/Sim%C3%B3n_Bol%C3%ADvar" title="Simón Bolívar">
        Simón Bolívar
       </a>
       , although this idea was shared by many contemporaneous, notably including
       <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_de_San_Mart%C3%ADn" title="José de San Martín">
        José de San Martín
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Bernardo_de_Monteagudo" title="Bernardo de Monteagudo">
        Bernardo de Monteagudo
       </a>
       , under either republican or constitutional monarchical governments. In 1826, Bolívar summoned a conference to be held in Panama, which was to be known as the
       <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_Panama" title="Congress of Panama">
        "Amphictyonic" Congress of Panama
       </a>
       because of the parallelism with the Hellenic
       <a href="/wiki/Amphictyonic_League" title="Amphictyonic League">
        Amphictyonic League
       </a>
       . The Congress was attended by
       <a href="/wiki/Gran_Colombia" title="Gran Colombia">
        Gran Colombia
       </a>
       (including present-day Colombia, Venezuela, Panama and Ecuador), the
       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Republic_of_Central_America" title="Federal Republic of Central America">
        Federal Republic of Central America
       </a>
       (including present-day Costa Rica, Nicaragua, El Salvador, Honduras and Guatemala), the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Mexican_States_(1824%E2%80%931864)" title="United Mexican States (1824–1864)">
        United Mexican States
       </a>
       , and Peru. The ostensible intention was to form a defensive league that could prevent foreign expansionism and foster the interests of the Spanish American republics. The Congress' conclusions, however, were not ratified by the participants, except for Gran Colombia. Soon after, both Gran Colombia and the United Provinces of Central America fell apart and the whole of Hispanic America was
       <a href="/wiki/Balkanization" title="Balkanization">
        balkanized
       </a>
       by competing national governments.
      </p>
      <p>
       By the 1990s, however, Brazil had consolidated as the most powerful country in South America (accounting for half of the regional GDP) and began to promote the notion of a united South America (a new regional framing) where Brasilia would be pivotal.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-academia.edu_17-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-academia.edu-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The project did not take hold until the United States' foreign policy priorities turned to other regions in the 2000s.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Formation">
        Formation
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Formation">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Cusco_Declaration" title="Cusco Declaration">
        Cusco Declaration
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Unasul_12.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1772" data-file-width="2480" height="157" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Unasul_12.jpg/220px-Unasul_12.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Unasul_12.jpg/330px-Unasul_12.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Unasul_12.jpg/440px-Unasul_12.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Unasul_12.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         South American presidents gathered during an extraordinary meeting for the signing of the
         <a href="/wiki/UNASUR_Constitutive_Treaty" title="UNASUR Constitutive Treaty">
          UNASUR Constitutive Treaty
         </a>
         in May 2008 in Brasilia.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The complete integration between the Andean Community and the
       <a href="/wiki/Mercosur" title="Mercosur">
        Mercosur
       </a>
       nations was formalized during the meeting of South American heads of state that took place on 23 May 2008 in
       <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">
        Brasília
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">
        <a href="#cite_note-18">
         [18]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       In the
       <a href="/wiki/2004_South_American_Summit" title="2004 South American Summit">
        2004 South American Summit
       </a>
       , representatives of twelve South American nations signed the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cuzco_Declaration" title="Cuzco Declaration">
        Cuzco Declaration
       </a>
       , a two-page letter of intent announcing the establishment of the then-named "South American Community of Nations". Panama and Mexico were present as observers. The leaders announced the intention of modeling the new community in the mold of the
       <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">
        European Union
       </a>
       , including a unified passport, a parliament and, eventually, a single currency. The then Secretary General of the Andean Community
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Allan_Wagner" title="Allan Wagner">
        Allan Wagner
       </a>
       speculated that an advanced union such as the EU should be possible within the next fifteen years.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Naming">
        Naming
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Naming">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_(2007).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1339" data-file-width="1776" height="166" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_%282007%29.jpg/220px-Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_%282007%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_%282007%29.jpg/330px-Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_%282007%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c2/Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_%282007%29.jpg/440px-Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_%282007%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kirchner-UN_General_Assembly_(2007).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/N%C3%A9stor_Kirchner" title="Néstor Kirchner">
          Néstor Kirchner
         </a>
         , first Secretary General of UNASUR
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       On 28 December 2005, Chilean former foreign minister Ignacio Walker proposed that the Union's former designation, the
       <b>
        South American Community of Nations
       </b>
       , abbreviated as
       <b>
        CSN
       </b>
       , be changed to
       <i>
        South American Union
       </i>
       ; nevertheless, many members stated to him that that proposal had already been rejected to prevent confusion since its acronym of U.S.A. (Spanish:
       <i>
        Unión Sudamericana
       </i>
       ) would be easily confused for the United States of America. In the press, the phrase "United States of South America" was bandied about as an
       <a href="/wiki/Analogy" title="Analogy">
        analogy
       </a>
       to the United States to reflect the economic and political power that the union would have on the world stage.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">
        <a href="#cite_note-19">
         [19]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">
        <a href="#cite_note-20">
         [20]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">
        <a href="#cite_note-21">
         [21]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">
        <a href="#cite_note-22">
         [22]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">
        <a href="#cite_note-23">
         [23]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">
        <a href="#cite_note-24">
         [24]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">
        <a href="#cite_note-25">
         [25]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The name was finally changed on 16 April 2007 to
       <i>
        Union of South American Nations
       </i>
       . The new name was jointly agreed by all member states during the first day of meeting at the First
       <a href="/wiki/South_American_Energy_Summit" title="South American Energy Summit">
        South American Energy Summit
       </a>
       ,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-terra1_26-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-terra1-26">
         [26]
        </a>
       </sup>
       held at
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Isla_Margarita" title="Isla Margarita">
        Isla Margarita
       </a>
       , Venezuela.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Structure">
        Structure
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Structure">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:UNASUR_(Ecuador).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2592" data-file-width="4608" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/UNASUR_%28Ecuador%29.jpg/220px-UNASUR_%28Ecuador%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/UNASUR_%28Ecuador%29.jpg/330px-UNASUR_%28Ecuador%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/UNASUR_%28Ecuador%29.jpg/440px-UNASUR_%28Ecuador%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:UNASUR_(Ecuador).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Headquarters of UNASUR
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The presidents of each member nation will have an annual meeting, which will be the top political mandate. The first meeting was held in
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brasilia" title="Brasilia">
        Brasilia
       </a>
       on 29 and 30 September 2005. The second meeting was held in
       <a href="/wiki/Cochabamba" title="Cochabamba">
        Cochabamba
       </a>
       , Bolivia, on 8 and 9 December 2006. The third meeting was held in Brasília – this meeting should have taken place in Indias (Colombia), but was postponed because of tension between Ecuador, Colombia and Venezuela. It was at this meeting that UNASUR was formalized and in which the
       <a href="/wiki/UNASUR_Constitutive_Treaty" title="UNASUR Constitutive Treaty">
        Constitutive Treaty
       </a>
       of the organization was signed.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">
        <a href="#cite_note-27">
         [27]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The foreign ministers of each country will meet once every six months. They will make concrete proposals for action and executive decision. The Permanent Representative Committee of the President of
       <a href="/wiki/Mercosur" title="Mercosur">
        Mercosur
       </a>
       and the Director of the Mercosur Department, the Secretary General of the
       <a href="/wiki/Andean_Community" title="Andean Community">
        Andean Community
       </a>
       , the Secretary General of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ALADI" title="ALADI">
        ALADI
       </a>
       and the Permanent Secretaries of any institution for regional cooperation and integration,
       <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Cooperation_Treaty_Organization" title="Amazon Cooperation Treaty Organization">
        Amazon Cooperation Treaty Organization
       </a>
       , Among others, will also attend these meetings.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">
        <a href="#cite_note-28">
         [28]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2017)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 9 December 2005, the Strategic Reflection Commission on the South American Integration Process was created. It consists of 12 members, whose function is to elaborate proposals that will help in the process of integration among the South American nations. These proposals were to be made at the 2nd UNASUR Meeting (2006).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">
        <a href="#cite_note-29">
         [29]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The Executive Committee, created at the 2nd UNASUR Meeting, was transformed into the Political Commission or Council of Deputies, in accordance with the Decisions of the Political Dialogue. The text prepared by heads of state to form UNASUR was approved at the 3rd UNASUR Meeting in Brasília on 23 May 2008. This meeting was scheduled to take place in Cartagena de Indias, Colombia, on 24–28 January 2008, but was postponed because of tensions between Ecuador, Colombia and Venezuela.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Secretary_General">
        Secretary General
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Secretary General">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Secretary_General_of_the_Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="Secretary General of the Union of South American Nations">
        Secretary General of the Union of South American Nations
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ernesto_Samper_(cropped).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1162" data-file-width="851" height="232" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Ernesto_Samper_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Ernesto_Samper_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Ernesto_Samper_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Ernesto_Samper_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/82/Ernesto_Samper_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Ernesto_Samper_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="170"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Ernesto_Samper_(cropped).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Ernesto_Samper" title="Ernesto Samper">
          Ernesto Samper
         </a>
         , the current
         <a href="/wiki/Secretary_General_of_the_Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="Secretary General of the Union of South American Nations">
          Secretary General
         </a>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       A Secretary General is the legal representative of the Secretariat in
       <a href="/wiki/Quito" title="Quito">
        Quito
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">
        Ecuador
       </a>
       . Former Ecuadorian president
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rodrigo_Borja" title="Rodrigo Borja">
        Rodrigo Borja
       </a>
       was nominated to this position but resigned a few days before the formation of the USAN in May 2008. On 4 May,
       <a href="/wiki/N%C3%A9stor_Kirchner" title="Néstor Kirchner">
        Néstor Kirchner
       </a>
       of Argentina was appointed as the first Secretary General, despite resistance from Colombia, Uruguay, and Peru. After the death of Néstor Kirchner in 2010, there was a period of time when the position went unfilled, which eventually ended when
       <a href="/wiki/Mar%C3%ADa_Emma_Mej%C3%ADa_V%C3%A9lez" title="María Emma Mejía Vélez">
        María Emma Mejía Vélez
       </a>
       was elected in March 2011.
      </p>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Presidency_pro_tempore">
        Presidency pro tempore
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Presidency pro tempore">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/President_pro_tempore_of_the_Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="President pro tempore of the Union of South American Nations">
        President pro tempore of the Union of South American Nations
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_(cropped).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3045" data-file-width="2214" height="234" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="170"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Presidente_Macri_en_el_Sillon_de_Rivadavia_(cropped).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Mauricio_Macri" title="Mauricio Macri">
          Mauricio Macri
         </a>
         , the current
         <a href="/wiki/President_pro_tempore_of_the_Union_of_South_American_Nations" title="President pro tempore of the Union of South American Nations">
          President of UNASUR
         </a>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The temporary presidency will be governed by a year and will be rotating among the member countries between each UNASUR meeting. They have already presided over UNASUR: Chile, from May 2008 to August 2009, Ecuador, from August 2009 to November 2010. The current president of UNASUR is Mauricio Macri,
       <a href="/wiki/President_of_Argentina" title="President of Argentina">
        President of Argentina
       </a>
       . According to the document "Decisions of the Political Dialogue", which was signed during the 1st South American Energy Meeting, a permanent general cabinet will be created and headquartered in
       <a href="/wiki/Quito" title="Quito">
        Quito
       </a>
       , Ecuador.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Secretary-General2_30-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Secretary-General2-30">
         [30]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Councils_and_bodies">
        Councils and bodies
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Councils and bodies">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The organisations of UNASUR are:
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">
        <a href="#cite_note-31">

        <a href="#cite_note-33">
         [33]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Council_of_Heads_of_State_and_of_Government_of_Unasur&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Council of Heads of State and of Government of Unasur (page does not exist)">
         Council of Heads of State and of Government of Unasur
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_Pro_Tempore_of_UNASUR" title="President Pro Tempore of UNASUR">
         President Pro Tempore of UNASUR
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Council_of_Minister_of_External_Relationships_of_Unasur&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Council of Minister of External Relationships of Unasur (page does not exist)">
         Council of Minister of External Relationships of Unasur
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Council_of_Delegates_of_Unasur&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Council of Delegates of Unasur (page does not exist)">
         Council of Delegates of Unasur
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Secretary_General_of_UNASUR" title="Secretary General of UNASUR">
         Secretary General of UNASUR
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>

      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Council_of_Economy_and_Finance">
        Council of Economy and Finance
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Council of Economy and Finance">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:UNASUR,_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_(9623068687).jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3183" data-file-width="4774" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/UNASUR%2C_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_%289623068687%29.jpg/220px-UNASUR%2C_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_%289623068687%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/UNASUR%2C_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_%289623068687%29.jpg/330px-UNASUR%2C_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_%289623068687%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/22/UNASUR%2C_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_%289623068687%29.jpg/440px-UNASUR%2C_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_%289623068687%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:UNASUR,_Reuni%C3%B3n_Ordinaria_del_Consejo_de_Ministro_de_Relaciones_Exteriores_(9623068687).jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Meeting of Ministers of Foreign Affairs of the members of Unasur.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Economic and Financial Council of Unasur was established on 12 August 2011, in
       <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">
        Buenos Aires
       </a>
       , during a meeting of Finance Ministers and representatives of the Central Banks of the twelve countries of the region. Argentine Deputy Economy Minister Roberto Feletti said that the Council would study measures to strengthen regional trade in national currencies without the use of dollar. "We have reached an agreement on three axes of work and one of them is to move forward with multilateral payment mechanisms, to sustain trade and protect the volumes of reserves," Feletti said, noting that trade between countries in the region moves 120 billion dollars Yearly. "The use of national currencies, excluding the dollar, protects reserves and increases trade because there are lower transaction rates." He also detailed plans of the technical groups focused on the development and strengthening of Development Banks, such as the Andean Development Corporation (CAF) and the
       <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_the_South" title="Bank of the South">
        Bank of the South
       </a>
       . He explained that the technicians will review the Latin American Reserve Fund (FLAR), aiming at in order to give greater capacity to intervene to the governments of the bloc in case of speculative attacks against currency or
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sovereign_debt" title="Sovereign debt">
        sovereign debt
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">
        <a href="#cite_note-35">
         [35]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Council_of_South_American_Defense">
        Council of South American Defense
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Council of South American Defense">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Council_of_South_American_Defense" title="Council of South American Defense">
        Council of South American Defense
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1333" data-file-width="2000" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg/220px-Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg/330px-Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg/440px-Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Bandeiras_UNASUL.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Flags of the member countries of UNASUR in front of the headquarters of the organization, in Ecuador.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The creation of a
       <a href="/wiki/Council_of_South_American_Defense" title="Council of South American Defense">
        Council of South American Defense
       </a>
       was proposed by Brazil and discussed for the first time at a summit of the South American presidents in April 2008. The project was extensively discussed throughout 2008. The then Brazilian Defense Minister, Nelson Jobim, said in April 2008 that the Council would be formed after the "political" decision of the presidents who participated in the launch of the Union of South American Nations (UNASUR) on 23 May 2008.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">
        <a href="#cite_note-36">
         [36]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-G1_2008_37-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-G1_2008-37">
         [37]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On 15 December 2008, at the extraordinary UNASUR summit, the creation of the South American Defense Council was finally approved. The defense ministers of Argentina, Brazil, Uruguay, Paraguay, Bolivia, Colombia, Ecuador, Peru, Chile, Guyana, Suriname and Venezuela. The Defense Council is responsible for developing joint defense policies, promoting the exchange of personnel among the Armed Forces of each country, conducting joint military exercises, participating in United Nations peace operations, promoting the exchange of analyzes on the world defense scenarios and the integration of industrial bases of military equipment.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">
        <a href="#cite_note-38">
         [38]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">
        <a href="#cite_note-39">
         [39]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">
        <a href="#cite_note-40">
         [40]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="South_American_Council_of_Health">
        South American Council of Health
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: South American Council of Health">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/South_American_Council_of_Health" title="South American Council of Health">
        South American Council of Health
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/South_American_Council_of_Health" title="South American Council of Health">
        South American Council of Health
       </a>
       is a UNASUR body established and approved on 16 December 2008, which brings together health ministers of the member states to develop regional programs in the region. Area of public health to be jointly financed by the South American bloc, to coordinate the energy policy of Unasur.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">
        <a href="#cite_note-41">
         [41]
        </a>
       </sup>
       It was created by decision of the Heads of State and Government of UNASUR, meeting extraordinarily in the Coast of Sauipe,
       <a href="/wiki/Bahia" title="Bahia">
        Bahia
       </a>
       , Brazil in December 2008. It was finally constituted on 21 April 2009 in
       <a href="/wiki/Santiago" title="Santiago">
        Santiago
       </a>
       , Chile.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-G1_2008_37-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-G1_2008-37">
         [37]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       It is a permanent council composed of Ministers from
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNASUR" title="UNASUR">
        UNASUR
       </a>
       member countries. This body was created in order to constitute a space of integration concerning health, incorporating efforts and improvements from other mechanisms of regional integration, such as
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MERCOSUR" title="MERCOSUR">
        MERCOSUR
       </a>
       , ORAS CONHU and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ACTO" title="ACTO">
        ACTO
       </a>
       , to promote common policies and coordinated activities among member countries. It is also a consultation and consensus body concerning health, which intends to delve deeply into relevant themes and strengthen public policies aimed at improving the living conditions of the inhabitants of the South American continent.
      </p>
      <p>
       Since health is an essential right to all human beings and all societies, and it is also a vital component for the development of mankind, the Health Council seeks political and social acceptance regarding the issue, proposing health to be seen as an important booster of cooperation and integration of the bloc’s nations, intensifying the coordination of such nations and respecting diversity and interculturalism in the region.
      </p>
      <p>
       The Health Council aims to strengthen, by establishing a South American political institution with expertise in sanitary issues, the development of solutions to challenges that transcend national borders, developing values and mutual interests among the neighboring countries, thus facilitating the interaction of the Member States health authorities through the exchange of knowledge and technology in the region. The South American Health Council (SHC) is composed of the Health Ministries of Unasur Member States. In order to achieve the Council’s goals, the Coordinating Committee - responsible for preparing propositions of Agreements and Resolutions - was created. The Presidency of the Health Council is held by the Minister of Health of the country nominated for the Pro Tempore Presidency (PTP) of Unasur. It is in charge of coordinating the activities of all its bodies and managing the Technical Secretary. The Pro Tempore President has a two-year term that may be extended for another two years, being unconditionally succeeded by a president from a different country. The SHC is supported by the Technical Secretary in charge of the Pro Tempore Presidency (PTP) and two countries of the previous and following PTP, in order to ensure the continuity of works. It is technically supported by the South American Institute for Government in Health (
       <a href="/wiki/South_American_Institute_of_Government_in_Health" title="South American Institute of Government in Health">
        ISAGS
       </a>
       ). Additionally, it is composed of five Technical Groups 1- Health Surveillance and Response; 2- Development of Universal Health Systems; 3- Health Promotion and Action on Social Determinants; 4- Universal Access to Medicines; 5- Human Resources Development and Management) and six Structuring Networks (1- Network of National Institutes of Health (RINS); 2- Network of Health Technical Schools of UNASUR (RETS), 3- Network of National Institutions and Institutes of Cancer (RINC); 4- Network of Public Health Schools of Unasur (RESP); 5- Network of Disasters Risk Management; 6- Network of International Offices and International Cooperation in Health (REDSSUR-ORIS)
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
        <a href="#cite_note-42">
         [42]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The [[
       <a href="/wiki/South_American_Institute_of_Government_in_Health" title="South American Institute of Government in Health">
        South American Institute of Government in Health
       </a>
       ]] (ISAGS) of UNASUR is an intergovernmental entity of public character that has as main objective to promote the exchange, the critical reflection, the knowledge management and the generation of innovations in the field of Health policy and governance.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">
        <a href="#cite_note-43">
         [43]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Summits">
        Summits
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Summits">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:2010_Unasur_summit.JPG">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3748" data-file-width="5622" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/2010_Unasur_summit.JPG/220px-2010_Unasur_summit.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/2010_Unasur_summit.JPG/330px-2010_Unasur_summit.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/2010_Unasur_summit.JPG/440px-2010_Unasur_summit.JPG 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:2010_Unasur_summit.JPG" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         South American leaders during the
         <a href="/wiki/2010_South_American_Summit" title="2010 South American Summit">
          Unasur 4th Summit
         </a>
         , in
         <a href="/wiki/Georgetown,_Guyana" title="Georgetown, Guyana">
          Georgetown
         </a>
         , Guyana.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Unasur_Lima_4.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1940" data-file-width="2924" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Unasur_Lima_4.jpg/220px-Unasur_Lima_4.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Unasur_Lima_4.jpg/330px-Unasur_Lima_4.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Unasur_Lima_4.jpg/440px-Unasur_Lima_4.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Unasur_Lima_4.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         Heads of State at the
         <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=5th_UNASUR_Meeting&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="5th UNASUR Meeting (page does not exist)">
          5th UNASUR Meeting
         </a>
         in Lima, in Peru.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The first Union summit was held in Brasilia on 23 May 2008, in which the Constitutive Treaty was signed. Due to the political crisis that Bolivia faced, pro-tempore president Michelle Bachelet convened an emergency summit in Santiago, Chile, on 15 September 2008. The leaders of Argentina, Bolivia, Brazil and Brazil took part in this summit, in addition to President Michelle Bachelet, Colombia, Ecuador, Paraguay, Uruguay and Venezuela and the Secretary General of the OAS, José Miguel Insulza.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">
        <a href="#cite_note-44">
         [44]
        </a>
       </sup>
       After a six-hour meeting between the leaders in the Palacio de La Moneda, they finally declared their support for President Evo Morales's government and gave "its absolute support to Bolivia."
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">
        <a href="#cite_note-45">
         [45]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>

      <p>
       There have been other presidential
       <i>
        extraordinary meetings
       </i>
       , such as:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        May 2010:
        <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">
         Buenos Aires
        </a>
        , Argentina. Election of Néstor Kirchner as
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Secretary_General_of_UNASUR" title="Secretary General of UNASUR">
         Secretary General
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        September 2010: Buenos Aires, Argentina. Discussion of the
        <a href="/wiki/2010_Ecuador_crisis" title="2010 Ecuador crisis">
         2010 Ecuador crisis
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        December 2010:
        <a href="/wiki/Mar_del_Plata" title="Mar del Plata">
         Mar del Plata
        </a>
        , Argentina. Kirchner's successor after his death. (Concurring with the 20th
        <a href="/wiki/Ibero-American_Summit" title="Ibero-American Summit">
         Ibero-American Summit
        </a>
        )
       </li>
       <li>
        June 2012:
        <a href="/wiki/Mendoza,_Argentina" title="Mendoza, Argentina">
         Mendoza
        </a>
        , Argentina. Discussion on the
        <a href="/wiki/Impeachment_of_Fernando_Lugo" title="Impeachment of Fernando Lugo">
         Impeachment of Fernando Lugo
        </a>
        and suspension of Paraguay. (Concurring with the XLIII
        <a href="/wiki/Mercosur" title="Mercosur">
         Mercosur
        </a>
        presidential summit)
       </li>
       <li>
        April 2013: Lima, Peru. Recognition of contested
        <a href="/wiki/Venezuelan_presidential_election,_2013" title="Venezuelan presidential election, 2013">
         Venezuelan presidential elections
        </a>
        results.
        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Maduro_48-0">
         <a href="#cite_note-Maduro-48">
          [48]
         </a>
        </sup>
       </li>
       <li>
        July 2013:
        <a href="/wiki/Cochabamba" title="Cochabamba">
         Cochabamba
        </a>
        , Bolivia. Discussion on the
        <a href="/wiki/Evo_Morales" title="Evo Morales">
         Evo Morales
        </a>
        "kidnapping" incident in Europe (due to European/US suspicions that the Bolivian Presidential aircraft carried US fugitive
        <a href="/wiki/Edward_Snowden" title="Edward Snowden">
         Edward Snowden
        </a>
        .)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">
        Demographics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Demographics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Demographics_of_South_America" title="Demographics of South America">
        Demographics of South America
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       UNASUR countries has together 410 million inhabitants and a rate of population growth of about 0.6% per year. There are several demographics such as
       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_forest" title="Tropical forest">
        tropical forests
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Atacama_Desert" title="Atacama Desert">
        Atacama Desert
       </a>
       and the icy portions of
       <a href="/wiki/Patagonia" title="Patagonia">
        Patagonia
       </a>
       . On the other hand, the continent presents regions of high population density, such as the great urban centers. The population is formed by descendants of Europeans (mainly
       <a href="/wiki/Spaniards" title="Spaniards">
        Spaniards
       </a>
       , Portuguese and Italians),
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Africans" title="Africans">
        Africans
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Indigenous_peoples" title="Indigenous peoples">
        indigenous
       </a>
       . There is a high percentage of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mestizos" title="Mestizos">
        mestizos
       </a>
       that vary greatly in composition according to each place. There is also a minor population of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asians" title="Asians">
        Asians
       </a>
       , especially in Brazil. The two main languages are by far Spanish and Portuguese, followed by French, English and Dutch in smaller numbers. Economically, Brazil, Argentina and Colombia are the wealthiest and most developed nations in the continent.
      </p>

      <p>
       <br/>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Languages">
        Languages
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Languages">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tleft">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo,_Brasil.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2336" data-file-width="3504" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo%2C_Brasil.jpg/220px-Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo%2C_Brasil.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo%2C_Brasil.jpg/330px-Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo%2C_Brasil.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo%2C_Brasil.jpg/440px-Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo%2C_Brasil.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Interior_do_Museu_da_L%C3%ADngua_Portuguesa_em_S%C3%A3o_Paulo,_Brasil.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         <a href="/wiki/Museum_of_the_Portuguese_Language" title="Museum of the Portuguese Language">
          Museum of the Portuguese Language
         </a>
         in São Paulo. Portuguese is the most spoken language in South America.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Portuguese, Spanish, English and
       <a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">
        Dutch
       </a>
       are the official languages of UNASUR. Spanish is the official language of Argentina, Chile, Uruguay, Paraguay, Bolivia, Peru, Ecuador, Colombia and Venezuela. Portuguese is the official language of Brazil.
       <a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">
        Dutch
       </a>
       is the official language of Suriname; English is the official language of Guyana.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">
        <a href="#cite_note-49">
         [49]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Indigenous_languages_of_the_Americas" title="Indigenous languages of the Americas">
        Indigenous languages
       </a>
       of South America include
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quechua_languages" title="Quechua languages">
        Quechua
       </a>
       in Peru, Bolivia, Ecuador, Argentina, Chile and Colombia;
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wayuunaiki" title="Wayuunaiki">
        Wayuunaiki
       </a>
       in northern Colombia (
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/La_Guajira" title="La Guajira">
        La Guajira
       </a>
       ) and northwestern Venezuela (
       <a href="/wiki/Zulia" title="Zulia">
        Zulia
       </a>
       );
       <a href="/wiki/Guarani_language" title="Guarani language">
        Guaraní
       </a>
       in Paraguay and, to a much lesser extent, in Bolivia;
       <a href="/wiki/Aymara_language" title="Aymara language">
        Aymara
       </a>
       in Bolivia, Peru, and less often in Chile; and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mapudungun" title="Mapudungun">
        Mapudungun
       </a>
       is spoken in certain pockets of southern Chile and, more rarely, Argentina. At least three South American indigenous languages (Quechua, Aymara, and Guarani) are recognized along with Spanish as national languages.
      </p>
      <p>
       Other languages found in South America include,
       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Hindustani" title="Caribbean Hindustani">
        Hindustani
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Javanese_language" title="Javanese language">
        Javanese
       </a>
       in Suriname; Italian in Argentina, Brazil, Uruguay, Venezuela and Chile; and German in certain pockets of Argentina, Brazil, and Chile. German is also spoken in many regions of the southern states of Brazil,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Riograndenser_Hunsr%C3%BCckisch" title="Riograndenser Hunsrückisch">
        Riograndenser Hunsrückisch
       </a>
       being the most widely spoken German dialect in the country; among other Germanic dialects, a Brazilian form of
       <a href="/wiki/East_Pomeranian_dialect" title="East Pomeranian dialect">
        East Pomeranian
       </a>
       is also well represented and is experiencing a revival.
       <a href="/wiki/Welsh_language" title="Welsh language">
        Welsh
       </a>
       remains spoken and written in the historic towns of
       <a href="/wiki/Trelew" title="Trelew">
        Trelew
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Rawson,_Chubut" title="Rawson, Chubut">
        Rawson
       </a>
       in the Argentine
       <a href="/wiki/Patagonia" title="Patagonia">
        Patagonia
       </a>
       . There are also small clusters of Japanese-speakers in Brazil, Colombia and Peru. Arabic speakers, often of
       <a href="/wiki/Lebanese_people" title="Lebanese people">
        Lebanese
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Syrian_people" title="Syrian people">
        Syrian
       </a>
       , or
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Palestinian_people" title="Palestinian people">
        Palestinian
       </a>
       descent, can be found in Arab communities in Argentina, Colombia, Brazil, Venezuela and in Paraguay.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">
        <a href="#cite_note-50">
         [50]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">
        Religion
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Religion">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       An estimated 87% of South Americans are Christians
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">
        <a href="#cite_note-51">
         [51]
        </a>
       </sup>
       (69%
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" title="Roman Catholic">
        Roman Catholic
       </a>
       , 18% other Christian denominations mainly Traditional
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Protestants" title="Protestants">
        Protestants
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Evangelicals" title="Evangelicals">
        Evangelicals
       </a>
       but also
       <a href="/wiki/Orthodoxy" title="Orthodoxy">
        Orthodoxy
       </a>
       ), accounting for ca. 19% of Christians worldwide.
      </p>
      <p>
       Both
       <a href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires" title="Buenos Aires">
        Buenos Aires
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">
        São Paulo
       </a>
       figure among the largest
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jewish_population_by_urban_areas" title="Jewish population by urban areas">
        Jewish populations by urban area
       </a>
       . Argentina also has the largest number of Muslims in Latin America, around 500,000
      </p>
      <p>
       Japanese Buddhism,
       <a href="/wiki/Shinto" title="Shinto">
        Shinto-derived
       </a>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Japanese_New_Religions" title="Japanese New Religions">
        Japanese New Religions
       </a>
       are common in Brazil and Peru.
       <a href="/wiki/Korean_Confucianism" title="Korean Confucianism">
        Korean Confucianism
       </a>
       is especially found in Brazil while Chinese Buddhism and Chinese Confucianism is spread throughout the continent. Due to the immigration of Indonesian workers, Suriname and Guyana have a large Hindu and Muslim community. Also
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kardecism" title="Kardecism">
        Kardecist Spiritism
       </a>
       can be found in several countries along with
       <a href="/wiki/Afro-American_religion" title="Afro-American religion">
        Afro-American religions
       </a>
       .
      </p>

         <b>
          <span class="flagicon">
           <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="750" data-file-width="1100" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Bolivia.svg/22px-Flag_of_Bolivia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Bolivia.svg/34px-Flag_of_Bolivia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Bolivia.svg/44px-Flag_of_Bolivia.svg.png 2x" width="22"/>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">
        Economy
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Economy">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_South_America" title="Economy of South America">
        Economy of South America
       </a>
      </div>

          </a>

        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:180px;max-width:180px">
         <div class="thumbimage">

          </a>

         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Sembrado_de_soja_en_argentina.jpg/220px-Sembrado_de_soja_en_argentina.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Sembrado_de_soja_en_argentina.jpg/330px-Sembrado_de_soja_en_argentina.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Sembrado_de_soja_en_argentina.jpg/440px-Sembrado_de_soja_en_argentina.jpg 2x" width="220"/>

         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Province_of_Buenos_Aires" title="Province of Buenos Aires">
          province of Buenos Aires

         . Argentina is the third largest producer of soybeans in the world.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg">

        </a>

          Paraguaná Refinery Complex

         , considered the second largest and largest capacity in the world.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1536" data-file-width="2048" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg/220px-Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg/330px-Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg/440px-Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Boa_Viagem_Beach_-_Recife_-_Pernambuco_-_Brazil.jpg" title="Enlarge">
